***яловый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:яловый.html>я́ловый</a> (23513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%B2%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%EA%99%97%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%B2%D1%8B%D0%B8amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ꙗловыи (page does not exist)">ꙗловыи</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jalovyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jalovъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">barren, infertile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%B2%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яловый.html>я́ловый</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jálovyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>barren (of animals)</li>
<li>made of the hide of a young calf</li></ol>
<h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"><a href = vnd.unilang:морфологический.html>Морфологи́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> синтаксические <a href = vnd.unilang:свойство.html>сво́йства</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%B2%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=2" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:редактировать.html>Редакти́ровать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздел.html>разде́л</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:морфологический.html>Морфологи́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> синтаксические <a href = vnd.unilang:свойство.html>сво́йства</a>»"><a href = vnd.unilang:править.html>пра́вить</a></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ло<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́ма</a> (2211)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BC%D0%B0amp;action=editamp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́ма</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jama</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ama</i>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BC%D0%B0amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́ма</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jáma</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́мы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́м</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pit, hole (in the ground)</li>
<li>dungeon</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BC%D0%B0amp;action=editamp;section=8" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BC%D0%B0amp;action=editamp;section=9" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ям-</b>; суффикс: <b>-очк</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>.

***ямщик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ямщик.html>ямщи́к</a> (27124)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BC%D1%89%D0%B8%D0%BAamp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BC%D1%8C%D1%89%D0%B8%D0%BA%D1%8Aamp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ямьщикъ (page does not exist)">ямьщикъ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jamĭščikŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BC%D1%87%D1%8Bamp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ямчы (page does not exist)">ямчы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yamçı</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">yamçı</i>. Ending modified under the influence of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-щик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BC%D1%89%D0%B8%D0%BAamp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямщик.html>ямщи́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jamščík</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> | <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямщик.html>ямщика́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямщик.html>ямщики́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямщик.html>ямщико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>driver, coachman, charioteer, cabman, postilion engaged in transporting people and cargo by horse and carriage</li>
<li>Eurasian nuthatch <i>(Sitta europaea)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal jargon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fence; brothel keeper</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BD%D0%B2%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%B8%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BD%D0%B2%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%8Camp;action=editamp;section=5" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:январь.html>янва́рь</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">janvárʹ</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:январь.html>января́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:январь.html>январи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:январь.html>январе́й</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:янки.html>я́нки</a> (21651)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BD%D0%BA%D0%B8amp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Yankee</i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BD%D0%BA%D0%B8amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:янки.html>я́нки</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jánki</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> | <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> | <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Yankee</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:янтарь.html>янта́рь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jantárʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BD%D1%82%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%BD%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:янтарный.html>янта́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jantárnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> amber
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:янтарный.html>янта́рное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожерелье.html>ожере́лье</a></i> ― <i lang="Ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jantárnoje</b> ožerélʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>amber</b> necklace</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>amber <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">colour</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***янтарь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:янтарь.html>янта́рь</a> (23863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D0%BD%D1%82%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%8Camp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Possibly ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Phoenician_language" class="extiw" title="w:Phoenician language">Phoenician</a></span> <i class="Phnx mention" lang="phn"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%F0%90%A4%89%F0%90%A4%8D%F0%90%A4%95%F0%90%A4%93amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="𐤉𐤍𐤕𐤓 (page does not exist)">𐤉𐤍𐤕𐤓</a></i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Phn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yntr</span> <span class="ts mention-ts Latn">/yainitar/</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sea-resin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">gintaras</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">dzintars</i>.

</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:яр.html>яр</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> | (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1c | // | 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. | <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. | Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:также.html>та́кже</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> | <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 1a: <a href = vnd.unilang:яр.html>я́ры</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:яр.html>я́ров</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:яр.html>я́рам</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:яр.html>я́рами</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:яр.html>я́рах</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:местный.html>Местный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>паде́ж</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яр.html>я́ру</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> ‘берег’); <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яр.html>я́ру</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> ‘овраг’).

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нга</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jaránga</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B3%D0%B8amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нги</a> (page does not exist)"><a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нги</a></a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B3%D0%B8amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нги</a> (page does not exist)"><a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нги</a></a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B3amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нг</a> (page does not exist)"><a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нг</a></a></b>)

<ol><li>yaranga <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a rounded or conical tent of reindeer hide, the traditional mobile home of some nomadic indigenous peoples of Russia.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:яркий.html>я́ркий</a> (1244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BA%D0%B8%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%EA%99%97%D1%80%D1%8A%D0%BA%EA%99%91%D0%B8amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ꙗръкꙑи (page does not exist)">ꙗръкꙑи</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jarŭkyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?Title=Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/jar%D1%8Ak%D1%8Aamp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/jarъkъ (page does not exist)">*jarъkъ</a></i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jaro</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jarъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ъkъ</i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BA%D0%B8%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>bright</li></ol>

<h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"><a href = vnd.unilang:морфологический.html>Морфологи́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> синтаксические <a href = vnd.unilang:свойство.html>сво́йства</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BA%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8Camp;action=editamp;section=2" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:редактировать.html>Редакти́ровать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздел.html>разде́л</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:морфологический.html>Морфологи́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> синтаксические <a href = vnd.unilang:свойство.html>сво́йства</a>»"><a href = vnd.unilang:править.html>пра́вить</a></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

***ярлык.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлы́к</a> (16875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BB%D1%8B%D0%BAamp;action=editamp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BB%D1%8B%D0%B3amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ярлыг (page does not exist)">ярлыг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yarlığ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BB%D1%8B%D0%BAamp;action=editamp;section=5" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлы́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jarlýk</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлыка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлыки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлыко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yarligh <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a written decree in the Mongol Empire and its <a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Division_of_the_Mongol_Empire" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Division of the Mongol Empire">successor states</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1865</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9A%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%BF%D0%BE%D0%B2,_%D0%93%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%A4%D1%91%D0%B4%D0%BE%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:ru:<a href = vnd.unilang:карп.html>Ка́рпов</a>, Геннадий Фёдорович">Геннадій Карповъ (Gennady Karpov)</a>,  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очерк.html>О́черки</a> изъ исторіи россіиской <a href = vnd.unilang:церковный.html>церко́вной</a> іерархіи</span></cite>, Moscow:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Метрополитъ Петръ, такъ <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> какъ <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> другіе, ѣздилъ въ <a href = vnd.unilang:орда.html>Орду́</a>; подъ 1313 годомъ въ лѣтописи <a href = vnd.unilang:говориться.html>говори́тся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:князь.html>Князь</a> Великій Михаилъ Ярославичъ <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> съ нимъ Митрополитъ Петръ <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошли́</a> въ <a href = vnd.unilang:орда.html>Орду́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> въ Ордѣ Ханъ Узвекъ сѣлъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> обновилось, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> всѣ <a href = vnd.unilang:приходить.html>приходи́ли</a> въ <a href = vnd.unilang:орда.html>Орду́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлыки́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>бра́ли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a>. Митрополитъ Петръ былъ въ Ордѣ <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хан.html>Ха́на</a> въ <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>велико</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:честь.html>чести</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> отпущенъ былъ отъ <a href = vnd.unilang:хан.html>Ха́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> многою честію <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:управа.html>упра́вою</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:русь.html>Русь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> всѣ <a href = vnd.unilang:православный.html>Правосла́вные</a> Христіяне встрѣчали <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> многою <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достью</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="Ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Metropolit Petr, tak že kak i drugije, jězdil v Ordu; pod 1313 godom v lětopisi govorítsja, što Knjazʹ Velikij Mixail Jaroslavič i s nim Mitropolit Petr pošlí v Ordu, po tomu što v Ordě Xan Uzvek sěl, i vse obnovílosʹ, i vsě prixodíli v Ordu i <b>jarlykí</b> bráli, káždyj na svojó ímja. Mitropolít Petr byl v Ordě u Xana v veliko česti, i otpuščen byl ot Xana so mnógoju čestiju i uprávoju na Rusʹ, i vsě Pravoslavnyje Xristijane vstrěčali jevó po étomu so mnógoju rádostʹju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Metropolitan Peter, like the others, rode to the Horde; under the year 1313 in the records it is said that the Grand Prince Mikhail Yaroslavich and with him Metropolitan Peter went into the Horde, for in the Horde came to sit the Khan <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C3%96z_Beg_Khan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Öz Beg Khan">Öz Beg</a>, and all was renewed, and all went into the Horde and took <b>jarlygs</b>, every one on his name. Metropolitan Peter was in high honour in the Horde by the Khan and he with his board were released from the Khan with high honours to Rus, and all Orthodox Christians therefore met him with much glee.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

intelléktom. Tradiciónnyje opredelénija uže ustaréli, vedʹ raspoznavátʹ izobražénija i tekst, otvečátʹ na prostýje voprósy i dáže pisatʹ múzyku uméjut vse te že nejroseti. Odnáko módnyj termin býstro podxvatíli marketólogi, i tepérʹ <b>jarlýk</b> II aktívno primenjájetsja v prodvižénii mnógix perspektívnyx sɛrvisov/sérvisov.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">That said, experts do not completely understand what should be considered artificial intelligence. The traditional definition has obsolesced over time, for recognizing pictures and texts, answering plain questions, and even composing music are things that all neural networks can do. However, the fashionable term has caught on fast with marketers and now the <b>label</b> "AI" is actively employed in the promotion of many prospective services.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shortcut, quick-access button

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">jarmark</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Jahrmarkt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fair</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BC%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%BA%D0%B0amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмарка.html>я́рмарка</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jármarka</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмарка.html>я́рмарки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмарка.html>я́рмарки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмарка.html>я́рмарок</a></b>)

***ярмо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>ярмо́</a> (30617)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BC%D0%BEamp;action=editamp;section=8" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ꙗрьмъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jarĭmŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*arьmo</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*arьmъ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂er-</i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BC%D0%BEamp;action=editamp;section=10" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>ярмо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jarmó</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>ярма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>ярма</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>я́рм</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>yoke <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">wooden bar</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иго.html>и́го</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ígo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> burden
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бремя.html>бре́мя</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">brémja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжесть.html>тя́жесть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tjážestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярость.html>я́рость</a> (3276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8Camp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?Title=Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/jarost%D1%8Camp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/jarostь (page does not exist)">*jarostь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fury</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">járȏst</i>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jarъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">furious</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ostь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">abstract nominalizer</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8Camp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярость.html>я́рость</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">járostʹ</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярость.html>я́рости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярость.html>я́рости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярость.html>я́ростей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fury, rage, frenzy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8Camp;action=editamp;section=6" title="Edit section: Related terms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"><a href = vnd.unilang:морфологический.html>Морфологи́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> синтаксические <a href = vnd.unilang:свойство.html>сво́йства</a></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярус.html>я́рус</a> (13975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D1%83%D1%81amp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">jarðhús</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">underground room</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">jǫrð</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">earth, modern Icelandic jörð</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hús</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D1%83%D1%81amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярус.html>я́рус</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">járus</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярус.html>я́руса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярус.html>я́русы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярус.html>я́русов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tier (horizontal row)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">theater</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> circle (a curved upper tier of seats in a theater)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> geologic stage</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярый.html>я́рый</a> (15074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jarъ</i>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярый.html>я́рый</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">járyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%BF%D0%BE%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B5amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="поярее (page does not exist)">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)</a><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B5amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ярее (page does not exist)">ярее</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%BF%D0%BE%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="поярей (page does not exist)">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)</a><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ярей (page does not exist)">ярей</a></b>)

<ol><li>ardent</li>
<li>violent, furious, vehement</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=6" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jaro</i>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=7" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярый.html>я́рый</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">járyj</span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> | obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> spring, summer</li>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ярый.html>я́рые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пчела.html>пчёлы</a></i> ― <i lang="Ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>járyje</b> pčóly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the first swarm of bees this year</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"><a href = vnd.unilang:морфологический.html>Морфологи́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> синтаксические <a href = vnd.unilang:свойство.html>сво́йства</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=2" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:редактировать.html>Редакти́ровать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздел.html>разде́л</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:морфологический.html>Морфологи́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> синтаксические <a href = vnd.unilang:свойство.html>сво́йства</a>»"><a href = vnd.unilang:править.html>пра́вить</a></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>рый</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. | Зализняка | — 1a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> | — <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B5amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ярее (<a href = vnd.unilang:страница.html>страни́ца</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существовать.html>существу́ет</a>)">ярее</a>, ярей.</i>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ясли.html>я́сли</a> (14591)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BB%D0%B8amp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ꙗсли</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jasli</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jasli</i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BB%D0%B8amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ясли.html>я́сли</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jásli</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> | <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ясли.html>я́слей</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>nursery, crèche</li>
<li>crib</li>
<li>manger</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ясно.html>я́сно</a> (533)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%BEamp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ясный.html>я́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jásnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%BEamp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Adverb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ясно.html>я́сно</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jásno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ясно" lang="ru"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%BF%D0%BE%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%B5%D0%B5amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="пояснее (page does not exist)">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)</a><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%B5%D0%B5amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="яснее (page does not exist)">яснее</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ясно" lang="ru"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%BF%D0%BE%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%B5%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="поясней (page does not exist)">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)</a>ясней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>clearly</li>
<li>brightly</li>
<li>finely</li>
<li>limpidly</li>
<li>distinctly, evidently</li></ol>

</p>

</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8Camp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ясность.html>я́сность</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jásnostʹ</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ясность.html>я́сности</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>clarity, lucidity
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ясность.html>я́сность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́сли</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="Ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jásnostʹ</b> mýsli</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">lucidity of mind</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внести.html>внести́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ясность.html>я́сность</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="Ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vnestí <b>jásnostʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to make things clear; to put things right</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%B7%D0%B0%D0%BC%D0%BD%D1%91%D0%BC_%D0%B4%D0%BB%D1%8F_%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B8amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:замять.html>замнём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ясность.html>я́сности</a> (page does not exist)"><a href = vnd.unilang:замять.html>замнём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ясность.html>я́сности</a></a></i> ― <i lang="Ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zamnjóm dlja jásnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="/w/index.php?title=let%27s_give_this_topic_a_restamp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="let | s give this topic a rest (page does not exist)">let's give this topic a rest</a></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ясный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ясный.html>я́сный</a> (1337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ěsnъ</i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ясный.html>я́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jásnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%BF%D0%BE%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%B5%D0%B5amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="пояснее (page does not exist)">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)</a><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%B5%D0%B5amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="яснее (page does not exist)">яснее</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%BF%D0%BE%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%B5%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="поясней (page does not exist)">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)</a>ясней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>clear</li>
<li>bright</li>
<li>fine</li>
<li>limpid</li>
<li>discrete</li>
<li>evident</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D0%BD%D1%8B%D0%B9amp;action=editamp;section=6" title="Edit section: Synonyms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ясн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ястреб.html>я́стреб</a> (18922)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D1%82%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B1amp;action=editamp;section=7" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jastrębъ</i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%81%D1%82%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B1amp;action=editamp;section=9" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ястреб.html>я́стреб</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jástreb</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ястреб.html>я́стреба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ястреб.html>я́стреба</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ястреб.html>я́стребы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ястреб.html>я́стребов</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ястреб.html>я́стребов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hawk (a predatory bird)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hawk, warmonger</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> | (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1c① | // | 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. | <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. | Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ястреб-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ячмень.html>ячме́нь</a> (21946)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%87%D0%BC%D0%B5%D0%BD%D1%8Camp;action=editamp;section=8" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%A9%D1%87%D1%8C%D0%BD%D1%A3%D0%BD%D1%8Aamp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ѩчьнѣнъ (page does not exist)">ѩчьнѣнъ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jęčĭněnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*(j)ęčьmy</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀκοστή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akostḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">barley</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">acus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">needle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ahar</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">corn-ear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%87%D0%BC%D0%B5%D0%BD%D1%8Camp;action=editamp;section=10" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ячмень.html>ячме́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jačménʹ</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ячмень.html>ячменя́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ячмень.html>ячмени́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ячмень.html>ячмене́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stye (bacterial infection of the eyelash or eyelid)</li>
<li>barley (annual temperate grasses of the species <i>Hordeum vulgare</i>)</li>
<li>barley (the grain of annual temperate grasses of the species <i>Hordeum vulgare</i>, used in making beer and whisky and for soups, puddings, etc.)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*aščerъ</i>.

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%89%D0%B5%D1%80amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ящер.html>я́щер</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jáščer</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> | <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ящер.html>я́щера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ящер.html>я́щеры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ящер.html>я́щеров</a></b>)

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%89%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BA%D0%B0amp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

***ящик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ящик.html>я́щик</a> (853)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%89%D0%B8%D0%BAamp;action=editamp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%BA%D1%8Aamp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="аскъ (page does not exist)">аскъ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">askŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%EA%99%97%D1%81%D0%BA%D1%8Aamp;action=editamp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ꙗскъ (page does not exist)">ꙗскъ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="Orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jaskŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.Org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">askr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wooden vessel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">eski</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ashen box</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*askaz</i> for cognates
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D1%8F%D1%89%D0%B8%D0%BAamp;action=editamp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ящик.html>я́щик</a></strong> • (<span lang="Ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jáščik</span>) | <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> | <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ящик.html>я́щика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ящик.html>я́щики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ящик.html>я́щиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>box, case, chest</li>
<li>drawer <i>(in a table)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> | derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> idiot box, boob tube (TV set)</li></ol>
